sīhō vi paidiṇaṁ ciya gēṇhai sāmāiyaṁ sunicchayaō । paḍikamaṇaṁ kuṇai tahā dōsu vi saṁjhāsu uvauttō ||7||6734 ॥
aha kēttiē vi kālē hittu kayāṇagāī bahuyāiṁ । vaccai uttaradēsaṁ sāmaggijuēṇa satthēṇa ||8||6735 ॥
tattōya aḍavimajjhē satthō āvāsiō naītīrē । sīhēṇa vi parigahiyaṁ sāmaiyaṁ tattha ṭhāṇammi ॥ 9 ॥6736 ॥
ētthaṁtarammi sahasā samāgaō bahalamasagasaṁghāō । tēṇaṁ khañjatō sō satthō vi haḍapphaḍō jāō ||10||6737॥
tattō dhūmāīyaṁ satthō juttaṁ karēi masagāṇaṁ । sīhō vi mahāsattō acchai taha cēva khajjaṁtō ॥11॥6738 ॥
mēru vya nippakaṁpō sō sammaṁ sahai uggamuvasaggaṁ । dhammajjhāṇammi ḍiō jhāēi suṇiccalamaīō || 12 ||6739 ॥
aha tēhiṁ masaēhiṁ jāva imō pāḍiō mahākaṭṭē । tā dakkhiṇavāēṇaṁ āgaṁtuṁ pēlliyā masagā ||13||6740 ॥
mukkō uvasaggāō sāmaiyaṁ pāraē taō sīhō । khaṇamēttēṇa ya dēhaṁ sūṇaṁ savvaṁ pi ēyassa || 14 ||6741 ॥
kaihiṁ vi diṇēhiṁ jāyaṁ satthāvatthaṁ puṇō vi hu sarīraṁ । tattō ya jāi puraō jāva vasaṁtappurē pattō ॥ 15॥6742॥
vikkēūṇaṁ bhaṁḍaṁ āsāiya tattha bahuguṇaṁ lābhaṁ । valiō ya niyayadēsassa sammuhaṁ jāva puṇa pattō ॥ 16 ॥ 6743 ॥
niyayambhi nayarammiṁ tattha paviṭṭhō u mahavibhūīē । niyaē pāsāyavarē bhuṁjai tatthuttamaṁ sōkkhaṁ || 17 ||6744 ॥
ēvaṁ sō visayahaṁ bhuṁjittā pacchimammi kālammi । saṁlēhaṇaṁ vihēuṁ aṇasaṇavihiṇā divaṁ pattō ||18|| 6 745 ॥
1. sunicchaiō pā0 ।। 2. haḍaphaḍō kā0 ॥

tattō caviūṇa imō bahusōkkhaparaṁparēṇa mōkkhasuhaṁ । pāvissaī kamēṇaṁ daḍhasāmaiyāikaraṇāō " ॥ 99 ॥ 6746 ॥
dēsāvagāsiyavayaṁ bīyaṁ sikkhāvayaṁ muṇēyavvaṁ । disivayapamāṇasaṁkhēvakaraṇaō hōi vinnēyaṁ ॥ | 1 ||6747 ॥

ēttha ya puṇa vinnēyā aiyārā paṁca vaṇijā u । āṇavaṇammi paōgō pēsavaṇē cēva nāyavvō ॥ 3 ॥6749॥

" ētthēva ya bharahammi saṁkhaurē gaṁgadattavaranāmō । āsi vaṇī vikkhāō, aha'nnayā tēṇa gurupāsē ॥1॥ 6752 ॥
gahiō sāvagadhammō paṁcāṇuvvaya- guṇavvayāīō । pālēi niraiyāraṁ taṁ dhammaṁ dhammabuddhī || 2 || 6753॥
aha annayā kayāī tēṇaṁ dēsāvagāsiyaṁ gahiyaṁ । jaha 'gēhāō bāhiṁ na niggamō cēiyaṁ mōttuṁ' ॥3॥6754॥

ēgō mahaṁtasatthō mahagghabahupaṇiyapūriō pavarō । tattha gayāṇaṁ jāyai lābhō lakkhēhiṁ bhiṁtaṁ || 5 ||6756 ॥

pabhaṇai ya gaṁgadattō 'ajaṁ dēsāvagāsiyaṁ gahiyaṁ । tā ēhāmi na ahayaṁ, tumaṁ puṇō kuṇasu jaṁ jōgaṁ' ॥ 7 ॥ 6758 ॥
puṇaravi tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ 'mā ēvaṁ kuṇasu ajaṁ bhāī ! tumaṁ । jēṇa mahaṁtō lābhō, vayaṁ tu kallaṁ karējjāsi' ॥8॥6759 ॥
sō bhāi 'mitta ! mā jaṁpa ērisaṁ ēkkajammiō lābhō । vayapālaṇaṁ tu bhāuya ! jammē jammē suhaṁ dēi' || 9 || 6760॥
sō bhaṇai 'bhaṁjiūṇa vi pāyacchittāō sujjhaē pāvaṁ । lābhō puṇa hatthāō uttiṣṇō labbhaē kattha ?' ||10||6761 ॥
sō bhaṇai 'na mē kajaṁ jō vayabhaṁgēṇa labbhaē lābhō । jēṇa pasaṁsaṁti buhā maraṇaṁ, na uṇō u vayabhaṁgaṁ' ॥11॥ 6762 ॥
iyarō vi bhaṇai 'supurisa ! ajaṁ ēkkaṁ karēhi maha vayaṇaṁ' | ciṁtai ya gaṁgadaṁttō “dhiratthu lacchīē pāvāē ||12|| 6763 ॥
jīē luddhā jīvā vayabhaṁga pi hu na cēva gaṇayaṁti । bahusō vi bhannamāṇō jaha ēsō cēva vaṇiyasuō" ॥ 13 ॥6764 ॥
iya ciṁtiūṇa bhaṇiō sō vaṇiō tēṇa gaṁgadattēṇa । jaha 'bhāi ! pāṇanāsē vi nō vayaṁ kahavi khaṁḍēmi ॥ 14 ॥ 6765 ॥
kajaṁ na majjha atthēṇa, nēya annēṇa taha ya kēṇā'vi । ēvaṁ ciya maha kajaṁ jaṁ kijjā nikkalō dhammō ' ॥15 ॥6766 ॥
iya jāṇiūṇa ēsō viṇicchyaṁ tassa gaṁgadattassa । niggacchai vaṇiyasuō udvittā tassa gēhāō ॥ 16 ॥ 6767 ॥
ēsō vi va puṇē bīyammi diṇē gaō tahiṁ satthē । diṭṭu ca tattha bhaṁḍaṁ divvavasā akkhayaṁ cēva ||17|| 6768॥
vihiyā ya taō saṭṭī gahiūṇa kayāṇagaṁ asēsa pi । pattō niyayagihammiṁ jāō ya tahiṁ mahālābhō ॥18॥6769 ॥

pariciṁtiyaṁ ca tēṇaṁ " māhappaṁ savvamēva dhammassa । ēyaṁ jaṁ maha lābhō jiṇabhavaṇāīsu tā dēmi” ॥ 19 ॥6770॥
iya ciṁtiūṇa savvēsu tēṇa jiṇamaṁdirēsu pūyāō । vihiyāō tahā dāṇaṁ dinnaṁ savvassa saṁghassa ||20|| 6771॥

tattō ya tēṇa vihiyā savvā saṁlēhaṇā jahābhihiyā । pacchā aṇasaṇavihiṇā mariūṇaṁ suravarō jāō ||22|| 6773 ॥
caviūṇa taō kamasō pahāṇakulasaṁbhavō bhavēūṇa । pattō ṇivvāṇapurē jattha aṇataṁ mahāsōkkhaṁ" || 23 ||6774 ॥
dēsāvagāsiyamiṇaṁ didrutasamanniyaṁ tuha'kkhāyaṁ । pōsahavayaṁ iyāṇiṁ kahēmi saṁkhēvaō kiṁci || 1||6775 |

āhārapōsahō hōi tattha savvammi taha ya dēsammi । savvammi u nāyavvō cauvvihāhārauvavāsō || 3 ||6777॥

appaḍi- duppaḍi-lēhiya-sējjāsaṁthārayaṁ vivajrēi । apamajiya - dupamajjiyasējjāsaṁthārayaṁ taha ya ||10||6784 ॥
ēvaṁ ciya dugabhēyaṁ buccai uccāra pāsavaṇabhūmiṁ । jaṁ sammamaṇaṇupālaṇa uvavāsē paṁca iyārā ॥ 11॥6785 ॥
ētthaṁ pi hu diṭṭhataṁ bhaṇāmi jiṇacaṁdasāvayaṁ suṇasu । “atthi puraṁ pōrāṇaṁ supaiṭṭhē nāma supasiddhaṁ || 1 || 6786 ॥

tattha'nnō vihu nivasai jiṇacaṁdō nāma sāvaō pavarō। daḍhasammattā'ṇuvvaya-guṇavaya- sikkhāhiṁparikaliō ॥ 3 ॥ 6788 ॥

kaiyā vihu puṇa tēṇaṁ pavvadiṇē pōsahō pariggahiō । sō tammi ḍiō acchai dhammajjhāṇammi vaṭṭaṁtō ॥ 5 ॥ 6790॥
ēgāgī subhabhāvō pōsahasālāē majjhayārammi । ētthaṁtarammi diṭṭhō sahasā sakkēṇa sō kaha vi || 6 ||6791॥

ahavā vi hu jaṁ jaṁ ciya ruccai taṁ taṁ vihijjaē kajjaṁ । taṁ taṁ ciya jaṁpijjai, pahuttaṇaṁ tēṇa ramaṇīyaṁ ॥ 10 ॥6795 ॥
tā ajjēva ya gaṁtuṁ cālēmi imaṁ imāō dhammāō" । iya ciṁtiūṇa tiyasō ēi duyaṁ tassa pāsammi ॥ 11 ॥6796 ॥

kāūṇa sūramuiyaṁ bhagiṇīrūvēṇa tassa lāhaṇayaṁ । ghēttūṇaṁ saṁpattō pabhaṇaṛa jaha 'bhāi ! giṇhāhi ||12||6797 ॥
āsi tumaṁ pōsahiō ka tā tujjha kāraṇē ēyaṁ । āṇīyaṁ suvisiddhaṁ bhattaṁ, uvavisasu, bhuṁjāhi ॥ 13 ॥ 6798 ।।

kāūṇa mittarūvaṁ āgacchai varavilēvaṇaṁ ghēttuṁ । mahamahiyapavaragaṁdhaṁ jaṁ harai maṇaṁ muṇīṇaṁ pi ॥ 16 ॥ 6801 ॥

pupphāī imāī tahā sugaṁdhagaṁdhāī ghāṇasuhayāī । tujjha kaēṇaṁ ṇiddhaya ! tā gēṇhasu, kuṇasu sahalaṁ ' ti ॥18॥ 6803 ॥
jiṇacaṁdō vi tahēva ya jāṇittāṇaṁ ḍiō u tuhikkō । dēvō vi bhaṇai 'ṇiddhaya ! kiṁ maha ruṭuō tumaṁ ajja ॥ 19 ॥ 6804 ॥
khamasu maē jai kiṁcivi avaraddhaṁ tuha ayāṇamāṇēṇaṁ' । iya bhaṇiūṇaṁ laggai pāēsaṁ tassa saḍūḍhassa ||20||6805 ॥
ēva kaē vi hu nō dēi uttaraṁ jāva tāva saṁharai । rūvaṁ mittassa tayaṁ, karēi aha bhāriyārūvaṁ ॥ 21 ॥6806 ॥
nijataṁ ēgēṇaṁ purisēṇaṁ ai aṇajarūvēṇaṁ । dhāhāvēi taō sā 'hā ! dhāvasu nāha ! nāha ! ti ॥ 22 ॥6807॥

jaṁpai imā vi 'piyayama ! kiṁ tuha ēēṇa hōhī (hii) vaēṇa । jai tuha pēcchaṁtassa vi maha sīlaṁkhaṁḍaē ēsō ? ' ॥ 25॥6810॥
iya jaṁpiyāvasāṇē dēvō pāḍēi tassa taṁ puraō । dhāhāvētiṁ bahusō bhujaṁtiṁ daṁsaē pāvō ॥ 26 ॥ 6811 ॥
taṁ daṇa vi ēsō “uvasaggamimaṁ " ti bhāviuṁ cittē । na vi muyai dhammajhāṇaṁ puṇō vi tiyasō kuṇai ruvaṁ ॥ 27॥6812 ॥
varavaṇijārayasarisaṁ āgaṁtu jaṁpaē taō ēsō । 'sāhu ! mahaṁ rayaṇāī giṇhāhi mahaṁtamōllāī ॥ 28 ॥ 6813 ॥
ahayaṁ māṇikavaṭṭō vikkiṇaṇatthaṁ imāṇa iha pattō । appēṇa vi mōllēṇaṁ tujjha payacchāmi ēyāṇi ॥ 29 ॥ 6814 ॥
jamhā hu majjha jaṇagassa saṁtiō āgaō lahu purisō । jaṁpai ya tujjha jaṇayassa atthi naṇu kāraṇaṁkiṁci ॥30॥6815॥
tā sigdhaṁ ciya tumaē gaṁtavvaṁ ' tēṇa ūsugō ahayaṁ । mōllēṇa thōyaēṇa vi tujjha payacchāmi nibrbhataṁ ॥ 31 ॥6816 ॥
tā giṇhasu, mā maṁcasu, dāhiṁti imāṇi tujjha mahalābhaṁ' । ēvabhaṇiō vi nō jāva jacchaē uttaraṁ kiṁci ॥32॥6817॥
tō jōi nāṇēṇaṁ dēvō jā pēcchaē tayaṁ saḍūḍhaṁ । varadhammajjhāṇagayaṁ kuddhō ya surō visēsēṇa ॥ 33 ॥ 6818 ॥
gaya-sīha - pisāyāī paḍikūlē vi hu karēi uvasaggē । taha vi na khubbhai ēsō, tuṭṭhō hiyaē taō tiyasō ॥ 34 ॥ 6819 ॥
kāūṇa pavararūvaṁ calaṁtamaṇikuṁḍalaṁ suhārillaṁ । vaṁdai puṇō puṇō vi hu giramērisayaṁ payaṁpatō ॥35॥6820॥
'tujjha kayatthō jammō, tujjha suladdhaṁ ca māṇusattamiṇaṁ । jaṁ ēvaṁvidhammō na muyasi maraṇē vi jiṇadhammaṁ ॥ 36 ॥ 6821॥
kiṁca tumaṁ varasāvaya ! tiyasasamūhāṇa majjhayārammi । aiharisaninbharēṇa sakkēṇa pasaṁsiō ahiyaṁ ||37||6822 ॥

taṁ asaṁhaṁtō ahayaṁ parikkhaṇatthaṁ tuhaṁ ihaṁ pattō । tā taṁ khamēja majjha savvaṁ pi hu jaṁ kayaṁ tujhaṁ ||38|| 6823॥
bhaṇasu ya jaṁ tuha dijai kiṁci varaṁ jēṇa taṁ payacchāmi' । saḍūḍhō vi bhaṇai 'kiṁ tuha varamannaṁ daṁsaṇāō vi ॥ 39॥6824॥
annamiha atthi lōē ? tā pujjau majjha tiyasa ! annēṇa' । tiyasō vi bhaṇai 'sāvaya ! suradaṁsaṇamimamamōhaṁ ti ॥40॥6825॥
tā bhaṇasu kiṁpi sāvaya ! taṁ kāuṁ jēṇa jāmi niyaṭhāṇē' । āha imō 'jai ēvaṁ tō sāsaṇaunnaī kuṇasu' ॥41॥6826॥
dēvō vi hu tavvayaṇaṁ paḍivajjiya jāi jiṇavaragihēsu । niyaparivārasamēō karēi aṭṭhāhiyāmahimaṁ ||42 ||6827 ॥
kāūṇa taō pūyaṁ nāṇāvihajalaya-thalaya kusumēhiṁ । rahasavasapūriyaṁgō hārōtthayaraiyavacchyalō ||43||6828॥
barakaḍaya-tuḍiyarthabhiyabhuyajuyalō kuṁḍalullihiyagaṁḍō । mauḍakayadittasiraō vēllahalabhuō paṇaccēi ॥ 44 ॥ 6829 ॥
daṭṭūṇa ya nañcaṁtaṁ dēvaṁ aṭṭhāhiyaṁ ca jiṇabhavaṇē । sabbō vi nayaralōgō bāhiralōō ya jaṁpēi ॥45॥6830॥
'bhō bhō ! pēcchaha ēvaṁ acchariyaṁ sirijiṇidadhammassa । jaṁ dēvā vi hu ēvaṁ biṁbē pūyaṁti vadati ॥ 46 ॥ 6831 ॥
gāyaṁti ya, vāyaṁti ya, ubvēllabhuyā tahā paṇacaṁti । jiṇapaḍimāṇaṁ puraō pēcchaha bhō ! dhammamāhappaṁ ॥ 47 ॥ 6832॥
tā ēsō yi aikkō iha dhammō jiṇavariṁdapaṇṇattō । jēṇa tiyasā vi ēvaṁ kuṇaṁti aṭṭhāhiyāmahimaṁ' ॥ 48 ॥ 6833 ॥
ēvaṁ pasaṁsamuhalaṁ lōyaṁ daṭṭhūṇa jaṁpai surō vi । 'bhō ! bhō ! bhō ! puralōyā ! maha vayaṇaṁ avahiyā suṇaha ॥49॥6834 ॥

"pēcchaha kaha bahuyāō tinni vi ēyāō bhōyaṇakaēṇa । ēvaṁ maṁtaṁtīō maṇōrahēhiṁ aṇēgēhiṁ ||27|| 6878 ॥

jamabhiruiyaṁ, ēyāē puṇa cautthīē ukkharabaḍiḍaḍriḍhallayasōggarayamāiyaṁ annaṁ pi jamacaṁtamaṇiṭuṁ kayasaṇaṁ taṁ piṁ

"haṁta ! jama amhēhiṁ maṁtiyaṁ bhōyaṇaṁ tayaṁ cēva । amhāṇaṁ saṁjāyaṁ kēṇā'vi hu kāraṇavasēṇa ||32||6883 ||

tucchō kāyavyō' । sīlamaīē bhaṇiyaṁ - 'halā ! kimaṇēṇa bhōyaṇamaṇōrahēṇa ? jaō jai tumhēhiṁ maṇōja bhōjaṁ bhuttaṁ tahā

kiṁci jaṁpiyaṁ taṁ tumha sasuraēṇa bīyapāsaṭṭiēṇa savvaṁ nisāmiyaṁ, taō mēṁ aṁbāḍiūṇa ēyaṁ nirūviyaṁ' । tāhiṁ pi

"pēcchaha tāyaṁbāṇaṁ buddhīē pagarisattaṇaṁ jēṇa । ēvaṁvihaṁ pi itthīrayaṇaṁ ēvaṁ paribhaviyaṁ ॥ 35 ॥ 6886 ॥

bātāṁdōlitadīpa kuḍmaladalaprāyaḥ priyaiḥ saṁgamastannāstīha kimapyudāramanasāmāśāmivēśāspadaṁ ||37||
tallabdhvā manujēṣu janma vimalaṁ saṁprāpya dēśādikam, śrutvā śrījinacandravācamucitāṁ śrīmadgurūṇāṁ puraḥ ।
svādhīnē ca dhanē ca saṁgatavati svīyē kuṭumbē satām, yuktō dharmavidhāna ēva satataṁ kartuṁ mahānudyamaḥ ॥ 38॥
samyagjñānapuraḥsaraśca mahatāṁ dharmādaraḥ sammataḥ, prāyastacca jināgamādavikalaṁ saṁjāyatē dhīmatām ।
sarvaṁ lōkamavēkṣya śāntaviśadaprajñāprakarṣōdyamaṁ kālē sō'pi kalau nyavēsi munibhiḥ saṁghōttamaiḥ pustakē ॥ 39 ॥
cāritrabhāracaraṇāsahamānasēna paṁcaprakāraviṣayāmiṣalālasēna ।
pātrādidānamayadharmavatā tadēvaṁ lēkhyaṁ parigrahavatā gr̥hiṇā tadēva ॥40॥
ēvaṁ vicintya suciraṁ śrēyōrthaṁ svasya sāṁbarājyaśrīḥ । śrīśāntināthacaritasya pustakaṁ lēkhayāmāsa ॥41॥
viracitavicitrarēkhaṁ suvarṇapatrāvalīkalitaśōbham । yadbhāti karē viduṣāṁ kaṁkaṇamiva kīlikāramyam ॥42॥
rākāśītāṁśuśubhrasphuradamaladr̥śaḥ sarvavastuprakāśī samyagjñānapradīpastribhuvanabhavanābhyantarē bhāsamānaḥ ।
yāvanmōhāndhakāraṁ śamayati sakalaṁ pūritāśēṣadōṣam, tāvannandyānmunīndrairayamiha satataṁ pustakaḥ paṭhyamānaḥ ॥42॥
॥ iti ॥ śrī śubhaṁ bhūyāt ॥

dvitīyaṁ pariśiṣṭam
prastuta 'sirisaṁtināhacariya mantargatāni granthagatāni subhāṣitāni
aidulahā pavvajjā ēsā saṁsāramajjhayārammi । paḍiyāṇaṁ pāṇīṇaṁ jiṇidacaṁdēhi jā diṭṭhā || 2315 ||
aipabalapavaṇavihuṇiyadēulasihara'ggasaṁṭhiyadhaō vva । mahilāmaṇaṁ na ghēppaṛa, tā dhī dhī thīsahāvassa ||5061||
aisayāṇaṁ samaggāṇaṁ sīlaṁ kāraṇamīriyaṁ । thaṁbhiyā jēṇa sīlāō damayaṁtīē gayādaō ॥ 91 ॥
accaṁtakurūvāṇa vi narāṇa rūvaṁ varaṁ bhavē sīlaṁ । jaha ṇaṁdisēṇasāhū dēvāṇa vi dullahō jāō ॥88॥
aṇavarayajahicchiyasaṁpaḍaṁtabhōgēhiṁ lāliō jīvō । saggammi na uṇa tittī jalaṇassa va dāruniyarēṇa ॥5046 ||
aṇasaṇu tāsu pahillauṁ aṁgū, kammakhayaha jaṁ kāraṇu caṁgū । ūṇōyariya biiya paviyāraha, jahiṁ ūṇattaṇu niyaāhāra ||5569 ॥
adattacāēṇa bhavaṁti bhōgā, adattacāēṇa visiṭṭhajōgā । adattacāēṇa na hōi daṁḍō, adattacāēṇa bhavē supiṁḍō ||3318 ||
annaha paricitijjai saharisakaṁḍujjaē hiyaēṇa । pariṇamai annaha cciya kajjāraṁbhō vihivasē ||7132 ||
annahā ciṁtaī jīvō hāsa - tōsaparavvasō । annahā taṁ vihāḍē divvō paramavēriō ॥ 330 ॥
anyathaiva vicintyantē puruṣēṇa manōrathāḥ । daivāhitasadbhāvāḥ kāryāṇāṁ gatayō'nyathā ॥ 7131 ||
apariggaṇaṁ bhavaī suvittaṁ, apariggahēṇaṁ varavattha- pattaṁ । apariggahēṇaṁ dhaṇa - dhannariddhī, apariggahēṇaṁ tu kamēṇa siddhī ||3320||

avamāṇēi māṇāō māyaraṁ piyaraṁ guruṁ । tēsimavamāṇaṇāē u duggaiṁ vaccaē ṇarō ॥5113 ॥
asārō ēsa saṁsārō, savvadukkhāṇa ālaō । ēttha maccubhayaṁ ghōraṁ jāyaī caugaīsu vi ॥2232 ॥
āī kōhō bhavē tēsi savvā'ṇatthaṇibaṁdhaṇaṁ । hiyāhiyaṁ na yāṇāī jēṇa jīvō vasīkaō ॥5110॥
ājammaṁ ciya payaī ēsā iha hōi supurisajaṇāṇa । jaṁ duhiyaparajaṇāṇaṁ pāṇēhiṁ vi karahiṁ uvayāraṁ ॥ 4137||
āyāsa-pāyāla-vaṇaṁtarālē abbhuggayā maṁdapasappamāṇā । kittīlatā viddhimuvēi sammaṁ sittā tavēṇaṁ sujalappaṇaṁ ॥96॥
ihalōē āyāsaṁ ayasaṁ ca karaṁti guṇaviṇāsaṁ ca । pasavaṁti ya paralōē sārīra - maṇōgaē dukkhē ॥ 639 ॥
uvayārēhiṁ parō cciya ghēppai agghaṁti tē tarhi cēva । iyarammi paujjaṁtā nēhābhāvaṁ payāsēṁti ॥ 5051 ॥
ēgadivasaṁ pi jīvō pavvajjamuvāgaō aṇannamaṇō । jai vi ṇa pāvai mōkkhaṁ avassa vēmāṇiō hōi || 16819 ||
ēgadivasaṁ pi jīvō pālai jō savvaviraimaccatthaṁ । sō jai na vi lahai sivaṁ, mahiḍḍiō hōi tō dēvō ॥ 3463 ||
ēvaṁ māyā vi savvāṇaṁ aṇatthāṇaṁ ṇibaṁdhaṇaṁ । jīē vasīkaō pāṇī savvaṁ cēva ṇigūhai ॥ 5114 ||
kāurisāṇaṁ visamō visamasarō, nēya dhīrapurisāṇaṁ । maṁsammi khaggadhārā tiṇhā, na uṇāi vajjammi ||5045 ||
kāūṇaṁ pāṇavahaṁ jīvā paṁcēṁdiyāṇa jīvāṇa । nivaḍaṁti mahānaraē, bhāvēhi imaṁ sacittammi ॥ 3777৷৷
kāmadhēṇū jahā dēi dujjhamāṇī maṇicchiyaṁ । dēvacaṁdēhiṁ sūrīhiṁ vaṇṇiyā bhāvaṇā tahā ॥ 108॥
kāyavvō iha jattō viraīē uttamēhiṁ purisēhiṁ । jamhā viraī saggā - 'pavaggasaṁsaggasaṁjaṇaṇī ||3461||

chijjau sīsaṁ, aha hōu baṁdhaṇaṁ, cayau savvahā lacchī paḍivannapālaṇēsu purisāṇaṁ jaṁ hōī taṁ hōu || 2426 ॥
jaṁ ajjiyaṁ caritaṁ dēsūṇāē vi puvvakōḍīē । taṁ pi kasāiyamēttō nāsēi narō muhuttēṇa ॥5562 ||
jaṁ ajjiyaṁ samīkhallaēhiṁ tava - niyama - baṁbhamaiēhiṁ । mā hu tayaṁ kalahaṁtā, chaḍḍēhiha sāgapattēhiṁ ॥5563 ॥
jaṁ annāṇī kammaṁ khavēi bahuyāhiṁ vāsakōḍīhiṁ । taṁ nāṇī tihiṁ guttō khavēi ūsāsamēttēṇa ॥ 2288॥
jē iṁdiēhiṁ purisā na hōṁti maraṇē vi laṁpaḍasahāvā । tē mahamuṇiṇō vva daḍhaṁ na ya ummaggaṁ pavajjaṁti ॥2936॥
jaṁ uyaraṁ airuiraṁ vibhāviyaṁ mōhamōhiyamaṇēhiṁ । taṁ asuinivahasaṁpūriyaṁ va, kira kōṭṭhayaṁ muha || 5748 ||
jaṁ jaṁ kappai cittammi jīvō kajjaṁ maṇicchiyaṁ । taṁ taṁ saṁpāḍaē savvaṁ sīlaṁ kappahumōvamaṁ ॥ 93 ॥
jaṁ jammaṁtari kammu kiu jīvi asuhu maṇēṇa । taṁ cūrijjai nittulauṁ rasamasatavalōḍhēṇa ||3736||
jaṁ pi muhaṁ airammaṁ visadr̥kaṁdōṭṭasacchahaṁ kaliyaṁ । taṁ pi galaṁtayalālākarāliyaṁ kiṁ na bhāvēha ? ॥ 5746 ॥
jaṁ pi varaṁgaṁ ṇīsēsavisayarasasuhasamūhayaṁ muṇiyaṁ । taṁ bībhacchaṁ asuīpavāhanijjharaṇamii muṇasu ॥5750 ॥
jai jīviyaṁ pi dijjai rāyaṇurattēṇa kēṇa vi ṇarēṇa । nārī tahavi ṇa ghippai, tā dhī dhī thīsahāvassa ॥5059॥
jai nēcchasi paḍiuṁ jē saṁsāramahāsamuddamajjhammi | navajāṇavattasarisaṁ tō pavvajjaṁ pavajjāhi ॥2711॥
jai nēcchasi nivaḍēuṁ saṁsāramahāgahīrakūvammi । navadaḍharajjusaricchaṁ tō pavvajjaṁ pavajjāhi ॥ 2712 ||
jai nēcchasi vasiuṁ jē bhavaguttiharammi bhīsaṇatarammi । tassugghāḍaṇavijjaṁ tō pavvajjaṁ pavajjāhi ॥ 2713||

jai nēcchasi ijjhēuṁ saṁsāramahādava'ggijālāhiṁ । navadōṇamēhatullaṁ tō pavvajjaṁ pavajjāhi ॥ 2714 ||
jaṛa nēcchasi bhamaḍēuṁ saṁsāramahārahaṭṭajaṁtammi । tabbhaṁgalōhadaṁḍaṁ tō pavvajjaṁ pavajjāhi ॥ 2715॥

jai nēcchasi viṇivāyaṁ saṁsāramahāḍavīē bhīmāē । bhavasayasahassadulahaṁ tō pavvajjaṁ pavajjāhi ॥ 2710 ।।
jai pavisai pāyālē, ciṭṭhai lōhassa paṁjarē vā vi । rukkha'ggē vā duruhai tahā vi chuṭṭai na dēvvāō ||2216 ॥
jai vā vaccai dūraṁ caittu dēsaṁtarāī bhayabhīō । tattha vi puvvakayāī puraō gaṁtūṇa ciṭṭhati ॥2217॥
jai sāyarammi pavisai mahallahalaṁtaraṁgirataraṁgē । tahavi na chuṭṭai kō vi hu saṁsārē puvvavihiyāō || 2214 ॥
jaidhammammi payattō kāyavvō niccamēva tubbhēhi । jamhā hu sāhudhammō dalēi nīsēsakammāī ||5653॥
jammaṁtarā'' vajjiyaduṭṭakammapāhāṇasaṁghāya'bhicūraṇammi । ṇimmāviō vajjasilācaēṇaṁ uggō tavō hōi ghaṇō mahaṁtō ॥ 98 ॥
jassa na bhatta'ṇuratā bhajjā samasuha- duhā gihē atthi । tassa gihaṁ pi hu rannaṁ abhaggavaṁtassa purisassa ॥7031॥
jassa puṇō pāsammi samasuha - dukkhā samāṇacittillā । atthi piyā guṇakaliyā raṇṇaṁ pi jaṇāulaṁ tassa ॥7032 ||
jaha kō vi rayaṇadīvē gaṁtuṁ laddhūṇa viviharayaṇāiṁ । niddapamāyapamattō hārai rayaṇāṇi maṁdamaī || 3886॥
taha jō laddhuṁ sammattamāivivihāraṁ dhammarayaṇāī । kuṇai pamāyaṁ mūḍhō sō hārai tāṇi nibdhaṁtaṁ ॥ 3887
jaha jalamajjhammi ṭhiyaṁ sasiṇō biṁbaṁ na tīraē ghēttuṁ । taha mahilāṇaṁ pi maṇaṁ, tā dhī dhī thīsahāvassa ||5060||

jahacitiyasaṁpajjaṁtasayalamaṇavaṁchiyāṇa ya surāṇa । ēkkaṁ ciya para dulahaṁ sīlaṁ nīsēsajayapayaḍaṁ ॥87॥৷
jahā u viddumaṁ sāraṁ sāgarāō bhavē tahā । bhīmāō bhavaō yāvi tahā sīlaṁ viyāhiyaṁ ॥ 92 ॥
jahā ṇarāṇaṁ iha kāmakuṁbhō bhavē sayā kāmiyakajjakārī । tahā tavō hōi maṇōgayāṇaṁ suhāṇa dāyā khalu tappamāṇō ॥ 101 ॥
jā kuṇai savvatati kammayarāṇaṁ tahēva baṁdhūṇa । uciyammi saṁpayaṭṭai gharassa lacchī, na sā ghariṇī ॥3240||
jā vi kaḍī suvisālā, mōhijjai jīē ēsa kira jīvō। sā haḍḍa-camma- maṁsēhiṁ ṇimmiyā, kiṁ na citēhi ? ॥ 5749 ॥
jā sā ahiṁsā paḍhamā vayāṇaṁ, sā bhāyaṇaṁ hōi sayā suhāṇaṁ । sā vajjatullā duhapavvayāṇaṁ, sā kāraṇaṁ sāsayasaṁpayāṇaṁ ॥ 3315 ॥
jāō vi ya jaṁghāō, kayalīthaṁbhōvamāō kaliyāō । ciṁtijjaṁtīō vivēiṇā u, tāō vi asuhāō ॥ 5751 ||
jāṇa kaēṇaṁ appā jala-jalaṇāīsu ghōrarūvēsu । pakkhippara aviyappaṁ tā dhī dhī thīsahāvassa ||5063 ||
jāva na rasamasakasamasahiṁ cūriu pāu tavēṇa । tāva ki labbhai daḍajiya jaṁ ciṁtiyā maṇēṇa || 3735 ।।
jīvā pamāyavasayā paḍaṁti saṁsārasāyarē ghōrē । tamhā tayaṁ vivajjaha, mā mujjhaha niyayakajjammi ||4858 ।।
jē uttamakulajāyā sumaraṁtā tē kulakkamaṁ dhīrā । mattagayaṁda vva sayā na ya ummaggaṁ pavajrjjati ॥ 2933॥
jē uttamajāīē saṁbhūyā hōṁti māṇavā kēi । jaccaturaya vva niccaṁ na ya ummaggaṁ pavajjati ॥ 2934 ॥
jē kaṇayakummasarisā pāyā varakāmiṇīṇa parikaliyā । tē aṭṭhipaṁjaramayā jīva ! tumaṁ dharasu cittammi ॥5752 ||
jē kuṁdakaliyavarapaṁtisacchahā manniyā imē dasaṇā । tē haḍḍakhaṁḍamālaṁ, paccakkhaṁ muṇasu rē jīva || 5745 ॥

*****
* jē kēi lōyammi guṇā pasatthā dīsaṁti jīvāṇa hiēkkakārī । nissēsayāṇaṁ pi tavappahāṇī ṭhāṇaṁ bhavē tāṇa narō paḍō vva ॥ 100 ॥
jē niyakajjaṁ mōttuṁ kuṇaṁti parakajjamēva aṇudiyahaṁ । kira supurisāṇa tāṇaṁ kō ṇu samō hōu puhavīē ? || 1557||
jē bīhaṁti sayā vihu jaṇāvavāyassa suddhaniyacittā । tē paṁḍiya vva purisā na ya ummaggaṁ pavajrjjati ॥ 2937॥
jē hōṁti uttamanarā uttamapayaittaṇēṇa tē niyayaṁ । aṁgīkuṇaṁti maraṇaṁ, na ya ummaggaṁ pavajjati ॥ 2932 ॥
*****
jē hōṁti mahāsattā payaīē cēva uttamattēṇa । tē jalanihiṇō vva sayā na ya ummaggaṁ pavajjaṁti ॥ 2935 ॥
|
jēmēi savvajimiē, suyai pasuttammi pariyaṇē savvē । paḍhamaṁ cēva viujjhai gharassa lacchī, na sā ghariṇī ॥3239 ॥
jēhi samaṁ paccūsē kīlijjai haṇibbharamaṇēhiṁ । tē vi diṇaṁtē rujjaṁti virasa - akaṁdasaddēhiṁ ॥ 2490 ॥
jō tappara uggatavaṁ mahappā nissaṁgacittō bhavabhīyagattō । sō dēvalōyāhivaīhiṁ ṇiccaṁ vaṁdijjaē bhattibharōṇaēhi ॥97॥
jō pāvō aṇubaṁdhaṁ na muyai viusēhiṁ bhannamāṇō vi । sō bhamaḍai saṁsārē aṇōrapārē samuddē va ||3398 ॥
ṇaya vijjāvihīṇassa sōhaē guṇasaṁpayā । jahā sōhaggahīṇāē ṇārīē rūvamāiyaṁ ॥ 314 ॥
ṇa hōi savvalōē vi jaṇō vīsāsabhāyaṇaṁ । dukkhāiṁ ṇēgarūvāī tahā māyāē pāvaī ॥5115 ॥
ṇārayā dukkhasaṁtattā jē ciṭṭhēti ṇiraṁtaraṁ । ṇiyaāukkhaē tē vi uvvaṭṭaṁti ṇiraṁtaraṁ ||2233||
* ṇimmalakaṁcaṇakalasa vva bhāviyā jē paōharā ruirā । avivēiṇā jaṇēṇaṁ, tē bhāvasu maṁsagurupiṁḍā ॥5747 ||
tattha vi ya savvaviraī pāvijjai guruyapuṇṇajōēṇa । tā tatthēva payattō kāyavvō buddhimaṁtēhi ॥ 633 ॥

bhattibharaṇibbharaṁgō jō varapattēsu viyara dāṇaṁ । sō sāsayasuhakaliyaṁ lahai ṇarō jhatti apavaggaṁ ॥ 82 ॥
bhāvaṇa suhamaṇakāraya, bhavasāyarataraṇa, duddamakaraṇaturaṁgahaṁ bhāvaṇa kayadamaṇa ।
sukkajhāṇauppāyaga, kēvalanāṇakara, kāmadhēṇu vara bhāvaṇa ēkka ji hōi para ॥102॥
bhāvaṇaṁ bhāvayaṁtassa suhāṇuṭṭhāṇakāriṇō । uppajjaē varaṁ nāṇaṁ lōyā'lōyappayāsayaṁ ॥ 107॥
bhāvaṇāē payaṭṭāṇaṁ ummaggaṁ jāi ṇō maṇaṁ । dhammaṭṭhāṇēsu savvēsuṁ suhēsuṁ saṁpayaṭṭaē ||103 ||
bhāvaṇāē suhāē u bhāviyāē ṇiraṁtaraṁ । sukkajjhāṇaṁ samārōhē ṇarō kammakkhayaṁkaraṁ ॥ 106 ॥
bhuvaṇaṁ pi bhūsiyamiṇaṁ sappurisēhiṁ na ēttha saṁdēhō । tēhi ciya supavittaṁ vihiyaṁ kiṁ vā viyappēṇa ? || 1558।।
bhō ! bhō ! ēsa rauddō aṇōrapārō mahābhavasamuddō । jammi visayā''misēṇaṁ bajjhati jiyā aṇimisa vva ॥ 755||
bhō bhō asārarūvē saṁsārē ēttha dukkhapaurammi । mā kijjau paḍibaṁdhī kuṇaha sayā ujjamaṁ dhammē ॥ 3884 ॥
bhōgā bahuvērakarā, alāhi bhōgēhiṁ pāvarūvēhiṁ । jāṇa kaēṇaṁ jīvā hiyāhiyaṁ nēva bujjhati ॥636 ॥
bhōgōvabhōgakaliō accharasāṇivahasaṁkulō rammō । jahacitiyadinnaphalō dāṇāō labbhaē saggō ॥ 81 ॥
maṁta-taṁtēhiṁ ṇō sakkā vārēuṁ ōsahēhiṁ vā । ṇa dhaṇēhiṁ, ṇa dēvēhiṁ, ṇa vējjēhiṁ, balēṇa vā ॥2237॥
maccū ṇiruvakkamō ēṁtō iṁdēhiṁ pi ṇa vāriō । sō kō vi ṇatthi saṁsārē maccuṇā jō ṇa pīḍiō || 2238 ||
majjēṇaṁ visaēhiṁ ya niddā - vigahāhiṁ mōhiyā jīvā । jē kēvi huṁti ētthaṁ lahaṁti tē bahuvihaaṇatthaṁ ॥ 4859॥

visayapamāyapamattā jīvā hiṁḍaṁti bhavakaḍillammi । jattha sarhati duhāī nāṇārūvāī ghōrāī ||4896 ॥
visayā siyāla - suṇagāiyāṇa savvāṇa hōṁti sāmannā । taha ṇidaṇijjarūvā uvviyaṇijjā buhagaṇāṇaṁ ॥757॥
visayāṇa sāhaṇāō nārīō hōṁti jīvalōgammi । ēvaṁvihāō tāō tā dhī dhī thīsahāvassa ॥ 5062॥
vihavu baṁdhaṇu maraṇu dāliddu dhaṇu pariyaṇu kitti jasu,
suhu vi dukkhu jaṁ jēṇa jaiyahaṁ pāvēvauṁ avasu phuḍu hōi tassa taṁ tēṇa taiyahaṁ ।
* jaṁ jasu kāraṇi jahiṁ vayasi jahiṁ maṁḍali jahi dēsī, vihibhaṁḍāriṇi ghaḍiu puṇu āṇai taṁ tasu rēsi ||2218||
****
viṣayatyāgē

nārīsvarūpē 615
bīyauṁ aṁgu viyāṇaha sīlaha, maddavu nāmēṁ niru parisīlaha । jahiṁ paṇāmu gōravvahaṁ kijjai, māṇaha niggahu jētthu vihijjai ॥5565 ॥ yatidharmē
vīsaṁbhajaṇiyagahiē parūḍhasabbhāvapēmmapasarammi । uvayārō kīrai māṇusammi kattōccayaṁ ēyaṁ ॥ 5054 ||
saṁsāraṇivvāṇasamubbhavāṇi sōkkhāṇi savvāṇi vi suṁdarāṇi । jīvassa āṇaṁdakarāṇi jāṇi tāṇaṁ pi hēū sutavō'ṇuciṇō ॥99॥
saṁsārammi asārē paribbhamaṁtāṇa ēttha jīvāṇa । sāsayasuhēkkamūlō jiṇadhammō dullahō vacchē ! ||632 ||
saṁsārasāyarō ghōrō apārō vi sarīriṇaṁ । bhāvaṇaṁ bhāvayaṁtāṇaṁ gōpayaṁ piva bhāsa ॥ 104 ॥
* saṁsārassa u mūlaṁ kōhāīyā u sōlasa kasāyā । jāṇa vasagō maṇussō bhamai mahābhavakaḍillami ॥ 1719||
sakkijjati ṇa ghēttuṁ uvayārēhiṁ vi aṇannasarisēhiṁ । rāmāō nāiṇī iva, tā dhī dhī thīsahāvassa ॥ 5058||

sanmārgē tāvadāstē prabhavati puruṣastāvadēvēndriyāṇām, lajjāṁ tāvadvidhattē vinayamapi samālambatē tāvadēva ।
bhrūcāpākṣēpamuktāḥ śravaṇapathayuṣō nīlapakṣmāṇa ētē yāvallīlāvatīnāṁ na hr̥di dhr̥timr̥ṣō dr̥ṣṭibāṇāḥ patanti ॥ 1916॥
sappurisacēṭṭhiyāṇaṁ mōllaṁ na hu atthi jīvalōgammi । jamhā supurisacēṭṭhā labbhai na hu davvasaṁkhāē || 1555 ॥
savvā vi hu pavvajjā pāyacchittaṁ bhavaṁtarakaḍāṇa । pāvāṇaṁ kammāṇaṁ tā jattō tattha kāyavvō ॥2488॥
savvāṇi mārīpamuhāṇi jāṇi duṭṭhāṇi jīvāṇa bhayaṁkarāṇi । bhattīē tattēṇa tavēṇa ṇiccaṁ khippaṁ viṇāsaṁ duriyāṇi jaṁti ॥ 95 ॥
sā dēi kallāṇaparaṁparāō, sā dāraē dāruṇaāvayāō । sā dēi saggammi suraṁgaṇāō, sā dēi mōkkhē suhasaṁpayāō ||3316 ॥
sīlu pavaru ābharaṇu sīlu tiyasāṇa vi dullahu, sīlu rūva-guṇaṇilau sīlu muṇijaṇamaṇavallahu ।
sīlu sayalaaisayasamaggu, bhavasāyaraviddumu, sīlatullu ṇa hu atthi ētthu tihuyaṇi kappahumu ॥85॥
sīhaha kēsara, saihi thaṇa, saraṇāiu suhaḍassa । maṇi matthai āsīvisaha na vi ghēppai amuyassa ॥7146 ॥
sutthēhiṁ dutthēhiṁ ya āvayapaḍiēhi taha apaḍiēhiṁ । dhammō cciya kāyavvō bhaṇiyamiṇaṁ jiṇavaridēhiṁ ॥ 7143॥
sō dhūlī hōi ṇarō, sō hu tiṇaṁ sō hu chārapuṁjō tti । jō avamāṇijjaṁtō sattūrhi vi ciṭṭhaī satthō ||856||
haṁtūṇaṁ parapāṇē appāṇaṁ jō karēi sappāṇaṁ । appāṇaṁ divasāṇaṁ karaṇa nāsēi appāṇaṁ ॥3772॥
hālāhalaṁ piva visaṁ jaha bhuttaṁ māraē ṇa saṁdēhō । taha ēē vi hu visayā māriti bhavē ṇa saṁdēhō ॥758 ॥
।

111 tamapr̥ṣṭhasyāntimapaṁktitaḥ 112 tama pr̥ṣṭhasyādimapaṁktatrayaparyantaḥ sandarbhaḥ dvi-dvicaraṇarūpāsu ṣaṭsu paṁktiṣu vibhaktavyaḥ ।
289 tamapr̥ṣṭhasya tr̥tīyapaṁktērārabdhaḥ saptamapaṁktigata kannu paryantaḥ caturdaśacaraṇātmakaḥ sandarbhaḥ dvi-dvicaraṇarūpāsu saptasu paṁktiṣu
vibhaktavyaḥ । tathā saptamapaṁktigata 'tikkhaṁkusu 'ityārabdhaḥ aṣṭamapaṁktigata rāyaṁgaṇaha 'paryantaḥ sandarbhaḥ apabhraṁśakāvyasya 'ghattā 'nāmakachandaḥ-
prakārasya pūrvārdharūpō jñēya:, tadanantaragataḥ aṣṭamapaṁktisandarbhaśca 'ghattā 'nāmakachandaḥ prakārasyōttarārdharūpō'vagantavyaḥ ।
